(f) every resolution adopted, budget passed, loan taken, assessment made, tax, fee or charge levied or imposed, improvement schemes framed, building plan sanctioned, license , permission or any other sanction granted, or standing orders made, or debenture or notice issued under the Municipal Act, 1911, or the Punjab Municipal Corporation Act, 1976 and in force at the commencement of this Act, shall be deemed to have been adopted, passed, taken, made, levied or imposed, framed, granted, sanctioned or issued under this Act, and shall unless altered, modified, cancelled, repealed, suspended, surrendered or withdrawn, as the case may be, under this Act, remain in force for the period, if any, for which it was so adopted, passed, taken, made, levied or imposed, framed, sanctioned, granted or issued; (g) all properties, movable or immovable, all rights of whatever kind used, enjoyed or possessed by, and all interests of whatever kind owned by or vested in,- (i) a Class I, Class II or Class III Municipal Council or a Nagar Panchayat, constituted under the Punjab Municipal Act, 1911, shall at the commencement of this Act, be deemed to be owned or vested in the Class ‘A’, Class ‘B’ or Class ‘C‘ Municipal Council or the Nagar Panchayat, as the case may be, as constituted under this Act; and (ii) the Corporation constituted under the Punjab Municipal Corporation Act, 1976, shall at the commencement of this Act, be deemed to be owned by, or vested in the Municipal Corporation, constituted under this Act; (h) all contracts made or liabilities incurred by, - (i) a Class-I, Class-II or Class-III Municipal Council or a Nagar Panchayat, constituted under the Punjab Municipal Act, 1911, and legally subsisting against the said Municipal Council, or the Nagar Panchayat shall, at the commencement of this Act, be deemed to have been made or incurred by the Class ‘A‘ Municipal Council, Class ‘B‘ Municipal Council or Class ‘C‘ Municipal Council or the Nagar Panchayat as the case may be, constituted under this Act; and (ii) the Corporation constituted under the Punjab Municipal Corporation Act, 1976, and legally subsisting against the said Corporation shall at the commencement of this Act, be deemed to have been made or incurred by the Municipal Corporation of the City constituted under this Act; (i) all Officers or other employees appointed under the Punjab Municipal Act, 1911, and the Punjab Municipal Corporation Act, 1976, and continuing in office immediately before the commencement of this Act, shall be deemed to have been appointed under this Act; (j) any assessment of lands and buildings made in respect of any ward or group of wards under the Punjab Municipal Act, 1911, or the Punjab Municipal Corporation Act, 1976, shall continue to remaing in force until assessment in respect of lands and buildings in respect of such ward or groups of wards is made under this Act and the payment of the tax on lands and buildings for any land or building for any quarter prior to the quarter commencing after the coming into force, of this Act, shall be made in accordance with the provisions of this Act; (k) any suit or other legal proceedings instituted or which but for the passing of the Act, would have been instituted by or against - (i) any Municipal Council or any Nagar Panchayat or any Executive Officer under the Punjab Municipal Act, 1911 may be continued or instituted by the Municipal Council or the Nagar Panchayat or the Executive Officer, as the case may be, constituted or appointed under this Act; and (ii) the Corporation or the Commissioner under the Punjab Municipal Corporation Act, 1976, may be continued or instituted by the Municipal Corporation or the Commissioner, as the case may be, constituted or appointed under this Act; and (l) all proceedings for acquisition of land initiated under the Punjab Municipal Act, 1911, or under the Punjab Municipal Corporation Act, 1976, whether in pursuance of any scheme of Improvement or otherwise, may be continued as if they had been initiated under this Act. (3) Notwithstanding the repeal of the Punjab Municipal (Executive Officer) Act, 1931, any appointment or contract made or any action taken under that Act, shall be deemed to have been made or taken under this Act.
Punjab Municipal Act, 1999_Section 601--> (1) If, any difficulty arises in giving effect to the provisions of this Act, the Government may by order published in the official Gazette make such provisions, not inconsistent with the provisions of this Act, as appear to it, to be necessary or expedient for removing the difficultly: Provided that no such order shall by made after the expiry of a period of two years from the date of coming into force of this Act. (2) Every order made under sub-section (1), shall, as soon as may be, after it is made, be laid before the Legislative Assembly of the State
Punjab Municipal Act, 1999_Section Sch.--> (See Section 114) Form of oath or affirmation Form of oath of office for a Mayor and President of a Municipality: "I, AB, having been elected as Mayor of the................Municipal Corporation/President of the......................... Municipal Council/Nagar Panchayat do hereby solemnly swear/affirm that I will bear true faith and allegiance to the Constitution of India as by law established, that I will uphold the sovereignty and integrity of India, that I will faithfully and consciously discharge my duties as the Mayor/President of the ................Municipal Corporation/Municipal Council/Nagar Panchayat and that I will do right to all people in accordance with Constitution and without fear or favour, affection or ill-will." II, Form of oath of a Member of Municipality: I, AB, having been elected a member of the................Municipal Corporation/Corporation/Municipal Council/Nagar Panchayat, do hereby solemnly swear/affirm that I will bear true faith and allegiance to the Constitution of India as by law established and that I will faithfully discharge the duties upon which I am about to enter.
Punjab Municipal Act, 1999_Section Sch.--> (See Sections 171 and 440) Amendments in the Land Acquisition Act, 1894, in its application to the State of Punjab in so far as they relate to acquisition of land by or for the Municipalities. 1. Amendment of section 4. - In the Land Acquisition Act, 1894 (hereinafter referred to as the principal Act), in section 4, after sub- section (2), the following sub-section shall be added, namely:- "(3) Notwithstanding anything contained in sub-section (1), the first publication of a notice of a Town Improvement Scheme or a Town Planning Scheme under sub-section (4) of section 436 of the Punjab Municipal Act, 1999, shall be substituted for and have the same effect as publication in the official Gazette and in the locality of a notification under sub-section (1) of section 4 of the principal Act except where a notification has previously been published under section 4 or a declaration under section 6, of the principal Act has previously been made and is still in force,." 2. Amendment of section 6. - In section 6 of the principal Act, after sub- section (3), the following sub-section shall be added, namely:- "(4) Notwithstanding anything contained in sub-section (1) or sub- section (2), the publication of the notification under section 438 of the Punjab Municipal Act, 1999, shall be substituted for and have the same effect as a declaration under section 6 of the principal Act unless a declaration under the said section 6 has previously been made and is still in force." 3. Amendment of section 11. - In section 11 of the principal Act, in sub- section (1),- (a) in clause (ii), the word "and" shall be omitted; (b) at the end of clause (iii), the word "and" shall be added; (c) after clause (iii), the following clause and proviso shall be inserted, namely:- "(iv) the costs which, in the opinion of the Collector, should be allowed to any person who is found to be entitled to compensation and who is not entitled to receive a sum of thirty percent of the market value, under sub- section (2) of section 23:" "Provided that the Collector may disallow wholly or in part the costs incurred by any person, if he considers that the claim made by such person for compensation, is extravagant," and (d) in the existing first proviso, for the words "provided that", the words "provided further that" shall be substituted. 4. Omission of Section 11-A. - Section 11-A of the principal Act, shall be omitted. 5. Amendment of section 15. - In section 15 of the principal Act, for the words and figures "sections 23 and 24", the words and figures, "sections 23, 24 and 24-A" shall be substituted. 6. Amendment of section 17. - In section 17 of the principal Act, - (a) in sub-section (3), for the word and figure "section 24", the words, letter and figures "sections 24 and 24-A" shall be substituted; and (b) after sub-section (4), the following sub-sections shall be added, namely:- "(5) sub-section (1) and (3) shall apply also to any area certified to be unhealthy by the Magistrate of the First Class. (c) before granting any such certificate, the Magistrate shall cause notice to be served as promptly as may be, on the persons referred to in sub- section (3) of section 9, and shall hear, without may avoidable delay, any objections which may be raised by such persons. (7) When proceedings have been taken under this section for the acquisition of any land, and any person sustains damage in consequence of being suddenly dispossessed of such land, compensation shall be paid to such person for such dispossession." 7. Insertion of new section 17-A - After section 17 of the principal Act, the following section shall be inserted, namely:- "17-A. Transfer of land to Municipality. - In every case referred to in section 16 or section 17, the Collector shall upon payment of the cost of acquisition, make over charge of the land to the Municipality, and the land shall there-upon vest in the Municipality subject to the liability of the Municipality to pay any further costs, which may be incurred on account of its acquisition." 8. Amendment of section 18. - In section 18 of the principal Act, in sub- section (1), for the words "persons interested", the words "persons interested or the amount of the costs allowed" shall be substituted. 9. Amendment of section 19. - In section 19 of the principal Act, in clause (c), after the words "amount of compensation", the words "or costs" shall be inserted. 10. Amendment of section 23. - In section 23 of the principal Act, - (a) in sub-section (1) - (i) in clause first, for the words, brackets and figures, "publication of the notification under section (4), sub-section (1)", the words, brackets and figures "publication of the notification under sub-section (4) of section 436 of the Punjab Municipal Act, 1999", shall be substituted; and (ii) in clause sixthly, for the words and figure "publication of the declaration under section 6", the words and figures, "publication of the notification under section 438 of the Punjab Municipal Act, 1999", shall be substituted; (b) to sub-section (2), the following proviso shall be added, namely:- "Provided that the provisions of this sub-section shall not apply to any land acquired under the Punjab Municipal Act, 1999,"; and (c) after sub-section (2), the following sub-section shall be added, namely; - "(3) For the purposes of clause first of sub-section (1) of this section: (a) the market-value of that land shall be the market-value according to use to which the land was put at the date with reference to which the market value is to be determined under that clause; (b) if it be shown that before such date, the owner of the land had in good faith taken active steps and incurred expenditure to secure a more profitable use of the same, further compensation based on his actual loss may be paid to him; (c) if any person after the publication of the notice under sub- section (4) of section 436 of the Punjab Municipal Act, 1999, without the permission of the Municipality, has erected, re-erected, added to or altered any building or wall, then any increase in the market-value resulting from such erection, re-erection, addition or alteration, shall be disregarded; (d) if the market-value had been increased by means of any improvement made by the owner or his predecessor-in-interest within two years before the aforesaid date, such increase shall be disregarded unless it be proved that the improvement so made was made in good faith and not in contemplation of proceedings for the acquisition of the land being taken under the Punjab Municipal Act, 1999; (e) if the market-value is specially high in consequence of the land being put to a use which is unlawful or contrary to public policy that use shall be disregarded, and the market value shall be deemed to be the market-value of the land, if put to ordinary use; and (f) when the owner of the land or building has after the passing of the Punjab Municipal Act, 1999, and within two years preceding the date with reference to which market-value is to be determined, made a return under any enactment in force of the rent of the land or building, the rent of the land or building shall not in any case be deemed to be greater than the rent shown in the latest return so made, save as the court may otherwise direct and the market-value may be determined on the basis of such rent: Provided that where any addition to, or improvement of, the land or building has been made after the date of such latest return and previous to the date with reference to which, the market-value is to be determined, the court may take into consideration any increase in the letting market-value of the land due to such addition or improvement." 11. Amendment of section 24. - In section 24 of the principal Act, for clause Seventhly, the following clause shall be substituted, namely:- "Seventhly, any outlay on additions or improvements of land acquired, which was incurred after the date with reference to which the market-value is to be determined unless such additions or improvements were necessary for the maintenance of any building in a proper state of repairs," or 12. In section of new section 24B After section 24-A of the principal Act, the following section shall be inserted, namely: "24B. Further provision for determining compensation. - In determining the amount of compensation to be awarded for any land acquired for the Municipality under this Act, the court shall also have regard to the following provisions, namely:- (a) When any interest in any land acquired under this Act has been acquired after the date with reference to which, the market value is to be determined, no separate estimate of the value of such interest shall be made so as to increase the amount of compensation to be paid for such land. (b) If, in the opinion of the court, any building is in a defective state, from a sanitary point of view, or is not in a reasonably good state of repair, the amount of compensation for such building shall not exceed the sum which the court considers the building would be worth, if it were put into a sanitary condition or into a reasonably good state of repair, as the case may be, minus the estimated cost of putting it into such condition or state. (c) If, in the opinion, of the court, any building which is used or is intended or is likely to be used for human habitation, is not reasonably capable of being made fit for human habitation, the amount of compensation for such building shall not exceed the value of the material of the building, minus the cost of demolishing the building." 13. Amendment of section 31 - In section 31 of the principal Act, - (a) in sub-section (1), after the word "compensation" the words "and costs, if any," shall be inserted; and (b) in sub-section (2), after the words "amount of the compensation", the words "or cost" shall be inserted. 14. Amendment of section 49. - In section 49 of the principal Act, to sub- section (1), the following Explanation shall be inserted, namely:- "Explanation. - For purposes of this sub-section land which is held with and attached to a house and is reasonably required for the enjoyment and use of the house, shall be deemed to be part of house."
Punjab Municipal Act, 1999_Section Sch.--> (See Section 458) Part I Purposes for which premises may not be used without a license . Carrying out of any of the following trades or operations connected with trades:- 1. Baking 2. Cinematograph films. Shooting of. 3. Cinematograph films by any process whatsoever. Treating of 4. Chillies or masala or corn or seeds. Grinding of by mechanical means. 5. Cloth, yarn or leather in indigo or in other colours. Dyeing or printing of. 6. Cloth or yarn. Bleaching. 7. Eating house or a catering establishment. Keeping of an. 8. Grain. Parching. 9. Groundnut seeds, tamarind seeds or any other sees. Parching. 10. Hairdrressing saloon or a barbar’s shop. Keeping of a. 11. Hides or skins, whether raw or dried. Tanning, pressing or packing. 12. Laundry shop. Keeping a. 13. Leather goods. Manufacturing of by mechanical means. 14. Litho Press. Keeping a. 15. Lodging house. Keeping of a. 16. Metal. Casting. 17. Precious metals. Refining of or recovering of them from embroideries. 18. Printing Press, Keeping a. 19. Punjab Municipal Act, 1999_Section Sch.--> Penalties (See sections 582 and 588) Fourth Schedule
Punjab Municipal Act, 1999_Section Sch.--> Regulations [See section 592] Subject to the provisions of this Act and the rules made there under the matters on which regulations may be made. A. Powers and functions of Mayor and President (Chapter VIII) Regulations relating to powers and functions of, - (a) the Mayor, under sub-section (1) of section 74; and (b) the President, under sub-section (1) of section 89. B. Conduct of Business (Chapter XI) Regulations relating to fixation of date and of time for holding meetings for the transaction of business under section 116. C. Borrowing (Chapter XIV) Regulations to carry out the purposes of Chapter XIV. D. Taxes (Chapter XVIII) Regulations relating to assessment and collection of taxes specified under sub-section (1), and levied under sub-section (2), of section 174. E. Assessment Code (Chapter XIX) Regulations relating to, - (a) the Municipal Assessment Code under sub-section (1) of section 182; and (b) the determination of fees under sub-section (5) of section 195 for recording transfer or devolution in the register. F. Advertisements (Chapter XXII) Regulations relating to, - (a) the form of, the manner in which, an application for a license or renewal of a license , under sub-section (2) of section 219 shall be made; (b) the determination of fees for the grant or renewal of a license under sub-section (3) of sectipn 219; and (c) the number of instalments and the manner in which tax on advertisement shall be payable under sub-section (3) of section 220. G. Recovery of taxes (Chapter XXV) Regulations relating to, - (a) the form of the notice of demand referred to in sub-section (1), and the fee to be paid for such notice of demand under sub-section (2), of section 242; (b) the form of the written notice referred to in sub-section (2) of section 244; and (c) the form of the warrant for attachment and sale of immovable property to be issued by the Chief Officer of the Municipality under sub- section (1) of section 246. H. Water Supply (Chapter XXVI) Regulations relating to, - (a) the terms and conditions for supply of water for other than domestic purposes under sub-section (1) of section 261; (b) the safety, maintenance and use of public hydrants or stand posts under subsection (3) of section 263; and (c) the form of the register to provide an inventory of tube wells under section 274, and the manner of maintenance thereof. I. Drainage and Sewerage (Chapter XXVII) Regulations relating to, - (a) the conditions for communication of private drains with the municipal drains for discharging foul water and surface water under sub- section (1) of section 306; (b) the discharge of trade effluent into municipal drains from trade premises under section 315; and (c) the permission for construction in any unsewered area of tank septic and sanitary privies and urinals and connection with septic tanks under section 319. J. Other regulations relating to water supply, sewerage and drainage (Chapter XXVIII). Regulations relating to, - (a) the exercise of power of the Chief Officer of the Municipality under sub-section (1) of section 322; (b) the time within which cause shall be shown under the first proviso to sub-section (1) of section 323; (c) the execution of work in relation to water supply, drainage and sewerage by the Municipality after giving an opportunity to the person liable to execute such work under sub-section (1) of section 325. (d) the power of the Chief Officer of the Municipality to erect upon any premises or affix to the outside of any building or to any tree any shaft or pipe; under section 326 for the purpose of ventilating any drain or cess pool; and (e) license s plumbers in respect of the following, namely:- (i) the exercise of adequate control on all license d plumbers; (ii) the inspection of all works carried out by such license d plumbers; and (iii) the hearing and disposal of complaints made by the owner or occupiers of premises with regard to the quality of work done, material used, delay in execution of work, and the charges made, by such license d plumber, under sub-section (8) of section 329; and (iv) generally for the guidance of such license d plumbers under sub- section (5) of section 329. K. Solid Wastes (Chapter XXIX) Regulations relating to solid wastes in respect of the following, namely:- (a) the determination of the class or classes of buildings in the case of which any building plan shall not be sanctioned except in conformity with the regulations for construction on the premises of receptacles for temporary deposit of solid wastes under sub-section (1) of section 347; (b) the types, materials of construction or design on the basis of which such receptacles, trailers or other means for removal of solid wastes may be constructed and where these may be located under sub-section (2) of section 347; and (c) the requirements of receptacles, trailers or other means for removal or for temporary deposit of solid wastes in premises used for the purpose specifiied in clause (a) or clause (b) or clause (c) or clause (d) or clause (e) of subsection (3) of section 347. L. Streets (Chapter XXX) Regulations relating to streets and public places in respect of the following, namely:- (a) the development, maintenance, control and regulations under sub- section (1) of section 351 of all public streets, parking areas, squares, sub-ways, over-bridges, parks and gardens vested in the Municipality; (b) the manner of publishing notice under the proviso to section 358 for giving reasonable opportunity to the residents likely to be affected by permanent closure of public street; (c) the determination of parking fees under sub-section (2) of section 361; (d) the defining of the regular line of a public street under sub- section (1), and the fee for inspection of the register and charge for taking extract therefrom, under sub-section (5) of section 363; and (e) the conditions of granting permission for any work referred to in section 380 and the deposit of money in advance for carrying out the work and restoring the street or pavement on which the work is carried out to its original condition under sub-section (1) of section 381. M. Building (Chapter XXXI and Chapter XXXII) Regulations relating to, - (a) the sanction or provisional sanction of refusal of building work under sub-section (2) of section 404; (b) the determination of cost of deputation under sub-section (5) of section 407; (c) the granting of permission for carrying building under sub- section (2) of section 411; and (d) the determination of the scale of fine for the area under unauthorized use under sub-section (4) of section 423. N. Planning (Chapter XXXIII) Regulations relating to the purposes for which entry may be made into or upon any land under sub-section (1) of section 442. O. Markets and Slaughter House (Chapter XXXIV) Regulations relating to, - (a) the approach roads or passage or pave, drain or light the same or such conveniences by the owner or the occupier or any license d private market, under sub-section (3) of section 451; (b) the expulsion of persons on the ground referred to in clause (a) of sub-section (1) of section 455; and (c) the inspection of places where unlawful slaughter of animals is suspected under sub-section (1) of section 457. P. License s (Chapter XXXV) Regulations relating to, - (a) the grant of municipal license for non-residential use of any premises under sub-section (1) of section 458, and the determination of the quantity of articles which may be stored in the premises for sale under the proviso to Section (2), the specification of different fees for different categories of non-residential use under sub-section (4), and display of license , inspection of premises and powers of inspector under sub-section (7), thereof; (b) the determination of fee for license under section 460; (c) the determination of fee for granting a municipal license to establish or keep open a private market under sub-section (1) of section 461; and (d) the determination of the procedure for the issue of license and its renewal under sub-section (3) of section 465. Q. Disposal of the dead (Chapter XXXVI) Regulations relating to the determination of fee for disposal of the carcass of a dead animal under sub-section (2) of section 478. R. Sanitation (Chapter XXXVIII) Regulations relating to, - (a) the inspection of premises for the purpose of ascertaining the sanitary condition under section 498; (b) the determination of fees under sub-section (2) of section 507 for the use of any place set apart under clause (a) of sub-section (1) thereof; and (c) the construction of any latrine or urinal for any premises under sub-section (1) of section 513. S. Urban Environment (Chapter XXXIX) Regulations relating to the removal, destruction, defacement, or otherwise obliteration of any notice or other document put up or exhibited under sub- clause (vii) of clause (a) of sub-section (1) of section 523. T. Procedure (Chapter XL) Regulations relating to, - (a) the fee for license on written permission referred to in sub- section (2) of section 530; (b) the compensation payable under sub-section (3) of section 532; (c) the time of entry under section 534; (d) the notices, bills, summons, orders, requisition or other documents required or authorized to be served under section 546 and section 543; and (e) the applications or appeals referred to in section 557. U. Miscellaneous (Chapter XLI) Regulation relating to any other co-related or incidental matter, for which regulations are required to be made or can be made.
Punjab Municipal Act, 1999_Section App.1--> Motion adopted by the Punjab Vidhan Sabha on the 22nd December, 1998. "That the Punjab Municipal Bill, 1998 be referred to a Select Committee, the Members of which be nominated by the Speaker, with a direction to make a report by the 15th March, 1999."
Punjab Municipal Act, 1999_Section App.2--> 1*Preliminary Report of the Select Committee on the Punjab Municipal Bill, 1998. 1. *Presented to the Punjab Vidhan Sabha on the 12th March, 1999. The select Committee on the Punjab Municipal Bill, 1998, as its meeting held on the 25th February, 1999, decided to request the Punjab Vidhan Sabha ?? extend the time for submission of its report on the Punjab Municipal Bill, 1998, by 1st March, 1999, as the Committee felt that it may not be able to finish its work by the stipulated date i.e. the 15th March, 1999. Balramji Dass Tandon, Chairman Minister for Local Government Punjab. Dated Chandigarh; The 10th March, 1999.
